    30	const MASK64 = 0xffffffffffffffffn
    31	
    32	function rotl(x: bigint, k: bigint): bigint {
    33	  return ((x << k) | (x >> (64n - k))) & 0xffffffffffffffffn
    34	}
    35	
    36	function wrappingMul(x: bigint, y: bigint) {
    37	  return (x * y) & MASK64
    38	}
    39	
    40	// xoroshiro128**
    41	export function xoroshiro128(state: bigint) {
    42	  return function () {
    43	    let s0 = BigInt(state & MASK64)
    44	    let s1 = BigInt((state >> 64n) & MASK64)
    45	
    46	    const result = wrappingMul(rotl(wrappingMul(s0, 5n), 7n), 9n)
    47	
    48	    s1 ^= s0
    49	    s0 = (rotl(s0, 24n) ^ s1 ^ (s1 << 16n)) & MASK64
    50	    s1 = rotl(s1, 37n)
    51	
    52	    state = (s1 << 64n) | s0
    53	
    54	    return result
    55	  }
    56	}

   903	            // if ep is legal, break and set the ep square in the FEN output
   904	            if (isLegal) {
   905	              epSquare = algebraic(this._epSquare)
   906	              break
   907	            }
   908	          }
   909	        }
   910	      }
   911	    }
   912	
   913	    return [
   914	      fen,
   915	      this._turn,
   916	      castling,
   917	      epSquare,
   918	      this._halfMoves,
   919	      this._moveNumber,
   920	    ].join(' ')

    30	const MASK64 = 0xffffffffffffffffn
    31	
    32	function rotl(x: bigint, k: bigint): bigint {
    33	  return ((x << k) | (x >> (64n - k))) & 0xffffffffffffffffn
    34	}
    35	
    36	function wrappingMul(x: bigint, y: bigint) {
    37	  return (x * y) & MASK64
    38	}
    39	
    40	// xoroshiro128**
    41	export function xoroshiro128(state: bigint) {
    42	  return function () {
    43	    let s0 = BigInt(state & MASK64)
    44	    let s1 = BigInt((state >> 64n) & MASK64)
    45	
    46	    const result = wrappingMul(rotl(wrappingMul(s0, 5n), 7n), 9n)
    47	
    48	    s1 ^= s0
    49	    s0 = (rotl(s0, 24n) ^ s1 ^ (s1 << 16n)) & MASK64
    50	    s1 = rotl(s1, 37n)
    51	
    52	    state = (s1 << 64n) | s0
    53	
    54	    return result
    55	  }
    56	}

    30	const MASK64 = 0xffffffffffffffffn
    31	
    32	function rotl(x: bigint, k: bigint): bigint {
    33	  return ((x << k) | (x >> (64n - k))) & 0xffffffffffffffffn
    34	}
    35	
    36	function wrappingMul(x: bigint, y: bigint) {
    37	  return (x * y) & MASK64
    38	}
    39	
    40	// xoroshiro128**
    41	export function xoroshiro128(state: bigint) {
    42	  return function () {
    43	    let s0 = BigInt(state & MASK64)
    44	    let s1 = BigInt((state >> 64n) & MASK64)
    45	
    46	    const result = wrappingMul(rotl(wrappingMul(s0, 5n), 7n), 9n)
    47	
    48	    s1 ^= s0
    49	    s0 = (rotl(s0, 24n) ^ s1 ^ (s1 << 16n)) & MASK64
    50	    s1 = rotl(s1, 37n)
    51	
    52	    state = (s1 << 64n) | s0
    53	
    54	    return result
    55	  }
    56	}

   121	
   122	export class Move {
   123	  color: Color
   124	  from: Square
   125	  to: Square
   126	  piece: PieceSymbol
   127	  captured?: PieceSymbol
   128	  promotion?: PieceSymbol
   129	
   130	  /**
   131	   * @deprecated This field is deprecated and will be removed in version 2.0.0.
   132	   * Please use move descriptor functions instead: `isCapture`, `isPromotion`,
   133	   * `isEnPassant`, `isKingsideCastle`, `isQueensideCastle`, `isCastle`, and
   134	   * `isBigPawn`
   135	   */
   136	  flags: string
   137	
   138	  san: string
   139	  lan: string
   140	  before: string
   141	  after: string
   142	
   143	  constructor(chess: Chess, internal: InternalMove) {
   144	    const { color, piece, from, to, flags, captured, promotion } = internal
   145	
   146	    const fromAlgebraic = algebraic(from)
   147	    const toAlgebraic = algebraic(to)
   148	
   149	    this.color = color
   150	    this.piece = piece
   151	    this.from = fromAlgebraic
   152	    this.to = toAlgebraic
   153	
   154	    /*
   155	     * HACK: The chess['_method']() calls below invoke private methods in the
   156	     * Chess class to generate SAN and FEN. It's a bit of a hack, but makes the
   157	     * code cleaner elsewhere.
   158	     */
   159	
   160	    this.san = chess['_moveToSan'](internal, chess['_moves']({ legal: true }))
   161	    this.lan = fromAlgebraic + toAlgebraic
   162	    this.before = chess.fen()
   163	
   164	    // Generate the FEN for the 'after' key
   165	    chess['_makeMove'](internal)
   166	    this.after = chess.fen()
   167	    chess['_undoMove']()
   168	
   169	    // Build the text representation of the move flags
   170	    this.flags = ''
   171	    for (const flag in BITS) {
   172	      if (BITS[flag] & flags) {
   173	        this.flags += FLAGS[flag]
   174	      }
   175	    }
   176	
   177	    if (captured) {
   178	      this.captured = captured
   179	    }
   180	
   181	    if (promotion) {
   182	      this.promotion = promotion
   183	      this.lan += promotion
   184	    }
   185	  }
   186	
   187	  isCapture() {
   188	    return this.flags.indexOf(FLAGS['CAPTURE']) > -1
   189	  }
   190	
   191	  isPromotion() {
   192	    return this.flags.indexOf(FLAGS['PROMOTION']) > -1
   193	  }
   194	
   195	  isEnPassant() {
   196	    return this.flags.indexOf(FLAGS['EP_CAPTURE']) > -1
   197	  }
   198	
   199	  isKingsideCastle() {
   200	    return this.flags.indexOf(FLAGS['KSIDE_CASTLE']) > -1
   201	  }
   202	
   203	  isQueensideCastle() {
   204	    return this.flags.indexOf(FLAGS['QSIDE_CASTLE']) > -1
   205	  }
   206	
   207	  isBigPawn() {
   208	    return this.flags.indexOf(FLAGS['BIG_PAWN']) > -1
   209	  }
   210	}

   303	
   304	/*
   305	 * NOTES ABOUT 0x88 MOVE GENERATION ALGORITHM
   306	 * ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
   307	 * From https://github.com/jhlywa/chess.js/issues/230
   308	 *
   309	 * A lot of people are confused when they first see the internal representation
   310	 * of chess.js. It uses the 0x88 Move Generation Algorithm which internally
   311	 * stores the board as an 8x16 array. This is purely for efficiency but has a
   312	 * couple of interesting benefits:
   313	 *
   314	 * 1. 0x88 offers a very inexpensive "off the board" check. Bitwise AND (&) any
   315	 *    square with 0x88, if the result is non-zero then the square is off the
   316	 *    board. For example, assuming a knight square A8 (0 in 0x88 notation),
   317	 *    there are 8 possible directions in which the knight can move. These
   318	 *    directions are relative to the 8x16 board and are stored in the
   319	 *    PIECE_OFFSETS map. One possible move is A8 - 18 (up one square, and two
   320	 *    squares to the left - which is off the board). 0 - 18 = -18 & 0x88 = 0x88
   321	 *    (because of two-complement representation of -18). The non-zero result
   322	 *    means the square is off the board and the move is illegal. Take the
   323	 *    opposite move (from A8 to C7), 0 + 18 = 18 & 0x88 = 0. A result of zero
   324	 *    means the square is on the board.
   325	 *
   326	 * 2. The relative distance (or difference) between two squares on a 8x16 board
   327	 *    is unique and can be used to inexpensively determine if a piece on a
   328	 *    square can attack any other arbitrary square. For example, let's see if a
   329	 *    pawn on E7 can attack E2. The difference between E7 (20) - E2 (100) is
   330	 *    -80. We add 119 to make the ATTACKS array index non-negative (because the
   331	 *    worst case difference is A8 - H1 = -119). The ATTACKS array contains a
   332	 *    bitmask of pieces that can attack from that distance and direction.
   333	 *    ATTACKS[-80 + 119=39] gives us 24 or 0b11000 in binary. Look at the
   334	 *    PIECE_MASKS map to determine the mask for a given piece type. In our pawn
   335	 *    example, we would check to see if 24 & 0x1 is non-zero, which it is
   336	 *    not. So, naturally, a pawn on E7 can't attack a piece on E2. However, a
   337	 *    rook can since 24 & 0x8 is non-zero. The only thing left to check is that
   338	 *    there are no blocking pieces between E7 and E2. That's where the RAYS
   339	 *    array comes in. It provides an offset (in this case 16) to add to E7 (20)
   340	 *    to check for blocking pieces. E7 (20) + 16 = E6 (36) + 16 = E5 (52) etc.
   341	 */
   342	
   343	// prettier-ignore
   344	// eslint-disable-next-line
   345	const Ox88: Record<Square, number> = {

   446	// Extracts the zero-based rank of an 0x88 square.
   447	function rank(square: number): number {
   448	  return square >> 4
   449	}
   450	
   451	// Extracts the zero-based file of an 0x88 square.
   452	function file(square: number): number {
   453	  return square & 0xf
   454	}
   455	
   456	function isDigit(c: string): boolean {
   457	  return '0123456789'.indexOf(c) !== -1
   458	}
   459	
   460	// Converts a 0x88 square to algebraic notation.
   461	function algebraic(square: number): Square {
   462	  const f = file(square)
   463	  const r = rank(square)
   464	  return ('abcdefgh'.substring(f, f + 1) +
   465	    '87654321'.substring(r, r + 1)) as Square
   466	}

   468	function swapColor(color: Color): Color {
   469	  return color === WHITE ? BLACK : WHITE
   470	}

   472	export function validateFen(fen: string): { ok: boolean; error?: string } {
   473	  // 1st criterion: 6 space-seperated fields?
   474	  const tokens = fen.split(/\s+/)
   475	  if (tokens.length !== 6) {
   476	    return {
   477	      ok: false,
   478	      error: 'Invalid FEN: must contain six space-delimited fields',
   479	    }
   480	  }
   481	
   482	  // 2nd criterion: move number field is a integer value > 0?
   483	  const moveNumber = parseInt(tokens[5], 10)
   484	  if (isNaN(moveNumber) || moveNumber <= 0) {
   485	    return {
   486	      ok: false,
   487	      error: 'Invalid FEN: move number must be a positive integer',
   488	    }
   489	  }
   490	
   491	  // 3rd criterion: half move counter is an integer >= 0?
   492	  const halfMoves = parseInt(tokens[4], 10)
   493	  if (isNaN(halfMoves) || halfMoves < 0) {
   494	    return {
   495	      ok: false,
   496	      error:
   497	        'Invalid FEN: half move counter number must be a non-negative integer',
   498	    }
   499	  }
   500	
   501	  // 4th criterion: 4th field is a valid e.p.-string?
   502	  if (!/^(-|[abcdefgh][36])$/.test(tokens[3])) {
   503	    return { ok: false, error: 'Invalid FEN: en-passant square is invalid' }
   504	  }
   505	
   506	  // 5th criterion: 3th field is a valid castle-string?
   507	  if (/[^kKqQ-]/.test(tokens[2])) {
   508	    return { ok: false, error: 'Invalid FEN: castling availability is invalid' }
   509	  }
   510	
   511	  // 6th criterion: 2nd field is "w" (white) or "b" (black)?
   512	  if (!/^(w|b)$/.test(tokens[1])) {
   513	    return { ok: false, error: 'Invalid FEN: side-to-move is invalid' }
   514	  }
   515	
   516	  // 7th criterion: 1st field contains 8 rows?
   517	  const rows = tokens[0].split('/')
   518	  if (rows.length !== 8) {
   519	    return {
   520	      ok: false,
   521	      error: "Invalid FEN: piece data does not contain 8 '/'-delimited <response clipped><NOTE>To save on context only part of this file has been shown to you.             // if ep is legal, break and set the ep square in the FEN output
            if (isLegal) {
              epSquare = algebraic(this._epSquare)
              break
            }
          }
        }
      }
    }`.

diff --git a/src/chess.ts b/src/chess.ts
index 8971fad..ed41251 100644
--- a/src/chess.ts
+++ b/src/chess.ts
@@ -813,6 +813,51 @@ export class Chess {
     this._incPositionCount()
   }
 
+  private _getEnPassantSquareAlgebraic(forceEnpassantSquare: boolean): string {
+    if (this._epSquare !== EMPTY) {
+      const square = this._epSquare
+      if (forceEnpassantSquare) {
+        return algebraic(square)
+      }
+      const bigPawnSquare = square + (this._turn === WHITE ? 16 : -16)
+      const squares = [bigPawnSquare + 1, bigPawnSquare - 1]
+
+      for (const s of squares) {
+        // is the square off the board?
+        if (s & 0x88) {
+          continue
+        }
+
+        const color = this._turn
+
+        // is there a pawn that can capture the epSquare?
+        if (
+          this._board[s]?.color === color &&
+          this._board[s]?.type === PAWN
+        ) {
+          // if the pawn makes an ep capture, does it leave its king in check?
+          this._makeMove({
+            color,
+            from: s,
+            to: square,
+            piece: PAWN,
+            captured: PAWN,
+            flags: BITS.EP_CAPTURE,
+          })
+          const isCheck = this._isKingAttacked(color)
+          this._undoMove()
+
+          // if ep is legal, break and set the ep square in the FEN output
+          if (!isCheck) {
+            return algebraic(square)
+          }
+        }
+      }
+    }
+
+    return '-'
+  }
+
   fen({
     forceEnpassantSquare = false,
   }: { forceEnpassantSquare?: boolean } = {}) {

@@ -813,6 +813,51 @@ export class Chess {
     this._incPositionCount()
   }
 
+  private _getEnPassantSquareAlgebraic(forceEnpassantSquare: boolean): string {
+    if (this._epSquare !== EMPTY) {
+      const square = this._epSquare
+      if (forceEnpassantSquare) {
+        return algebraic(square)
+      }
+      const bigPawnSquare = square + (this._turn === WHITE ? 16 : -16)
+      const squares = [bigPawnSquare + 1, bigPawnSquare - 1]
+
+      for (const s of squares) {
+        // is the square off the board?
+        if (s & 0x88) {
+          continue
+        }
+
+        const color = this._turn
+
+        // is there a pawn that can capture the epSquare?
+        if (
+          this._board[s]?.color === color &&
+          this._board[s]?.type === PAWN
+        ) {
+          // if the pawn makes an ep capture, does it leave its king in check?
+          this._makeMove({
+            color,
+            from: s,
+            to: square,
+            piece: PAWN,
+            captured: PAWN,
+            flags: BITS.EP_CAPTURE,
+          })
+          const isCheck = this._isKingAttacked(color)
+          this._undoMove()
+
+          // if ep is legal, break and set the ep square in the FEN output
+          if (!isCheck) {
+            return algebraic(square)
+          }
+        }
+      }
+    }
+
+    return '-'
+  }
+
